The legacy alerting engine (`AlertEngine`, `AlertService`, `DashAlertExtractor`, etc.) has been **completely removed** from this version of the codebase. Exhaustive searches for every known symbol returned zero results. The engine existed in Grafana ≤ 9.x and was deleted in a later major version.

---

### 2. Unified Alerting (ngalert) Engine — **4 files**

| File | Role |
|---|---|
| `pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go` | Top-level `AlertNG` service; wires together all subsystems via `ProvideService` / `Run` |
| `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go` | Scheduling engine — periodic tick loop, rule dispatch, lifecycle management |
| `pkg/services/ngalert/eval/eval.go` | Condition evaluation engine — builds expression pipelines, produces typed `Results` |
| `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/fetcher.go` | `updateSchedulableAlertRules` — computes add/update/delete diff for the scheduler |

---

### 3. Legacy Alert Rule Storage — **1 file (schema only)**

| File | Role |
|---|---|
| `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/alert_mig.go` | `addAlertMigrations` — DDL for the legacy `alert`, `alert_rule_tag`, `alert_notification`, `alert_notification_state` tables |

No runtime Go service for reading/writing legacy alert rows exists; only the schema migration survives for database upgrade continuity.

---

There may be files that are not used anymore.\", \"path\", alertingDir, \"files_to_delete\", keys, \"error\", err)\n                }\n        }\n\n        for _, entry := range entries {\n                _, known := knownFiles[entry.Name()]\n                if known {\n                        if orgId == 0 {\n                                deleteFile(entry.Name())\n                        } else {\n                                moveFile(entry.Name())\n                        }\n                }\n        }\n}\n\nfunc (u *upgradeNgAlerting) SQL(migrator.Dialect) string {\n        return codeMigration\n}"

  // if there are records with org_id == 0 then the feature flag was enabled before 8.2 that introduced org separation.\n        // if feature is enabled in 8.2 the migration \"AddDashAlertMigration\", which is effectively different from what was run in 8.1.x and earlier versions,\n        // will handle organizations correctly, and, therefore, nothing needs to be fixed\n err)\n        }\n        if count == 0 {\n                return 0, nil // NOTHING TO DO\n        }\n\n        orgs := make([]int64, 0)\n        // get all org IDs sorted in ascending order\n        if err = sess.Table(\"org\").OrderBy(\"id\").Cols(\"id\").Find(&orgs); err != nil {\n                return 0, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to query table org: %w\", err)\n        }\n        if len(orgs) == 0 { // should not really happen\n                migrator.Logger.Info(\"No organizations are found. Nothing to migrate\")\n                return 0, nil\n        }\n\n        firstOrg := orgs[0]\n\n        // assigning all configurations to the first org because 0 does not usually point to any\n        migrator.Logger.Info(\"Assigning all existing records from alert_configuration to the first organization\", \"org\", firstOrg)\n        _, err = sess.Cols(\"org_id\").Where(\"org_id = 0\").Update(&AlertConfiguration{OrgID: firstOrg})\n        if err != nil {\n                return 0, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to update org_id for all rows in the table alert_configuration: %w\", err)\n        }\n\n        // if there is a single organization it is safe to assume that all configurations belong to it.\n        if len(orgs) == 1 {\n                return firstOrg, nil\n        }\n        // if there are many organizations we cannot safely assume what organization an alert_configuration belongs to.\n        // Therefore, we apply the default configuration to all organizations. The previous version could be restored if needed.\n        migrator.Logger.Warn(\"Detected many organizations. The current alertmanager configuration will be replaced by the default one\")\n        configs := make([]*AlertConfiguration, 0, len(orgs))\n        for _, org := range orgs {\n                configs = append(configs, &AlertConfiguration{\n                        AlertmanagerConfiguration: migrator.Cfg.UnifiedAlerting.DefaultConfiguration,\n                        // Since we are migration for a snapshot of the code, it is always going to migrate to\n                        // the v1 config.\n                        ConfigurationVersion: \"v1\",\n                        OrgID:                org,\n                })\n        }\n\n        _, err = sess.InsertMulti(configs)\n        if err != nil {\n                return 0, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to add default alertmanager configurations to every organization: %w\", err)\n        }\n        return 0, nil\n}\n\n// updateAlertmanagerFiles scans the existing alerting directory '<data_dir>/alerting' for known files.\n// If argument 'orgId' is not 0 updateAlertmanagerFiles moves all known files to the directory <data_dir>/alerting/<orgId>.\n// Otherwise, it deletes those files.\n// pre-8.2 version put all configuration files into the root of alerting directory. Since 8.2 configuration files are put in organization specific directory\nfunc (u *upgradeNgAlerting) updateAlertmanagerFiles(orgId int64, migrator *migrator.Migrator) {\n        knownFiles := map[string]any{\"__default__.tmpl\": nil, \"silences\": nil, \"notifications\": nil}\n        alertingDir := filepath.Join(migrator.Cfg.DataPath, \"alerting\")\n\n        // do not fail if something goes wrong because these files are not used anymore. the worst that can happen is that we leave some leftovers behind\n        deleteFile := func(fileName string) {\n                path := filepath.Join(alertingDir, fileName)\n                migrator.Logger.Info(\"Deleting alerting configuration file\", \"file\", fileName)\n                err := os.Remove(path)\n                if err != nil {\n                        migrator.Logger.Warn(\"Failed to delete file\", \"file\", path, \"error\", err)\n                }\n        }\n\n        moveFile := func(fileName string) {\n                alertingOrgDir := filepath.Join(alertingDir, strconv.FormatInt(orgId, 10))\n                if err := os.MkdirAll(alertingOrgDir, 0750); err != nil {\n                        migrator.Logger.Error(\"Failed to create alerting directory for organization. Skip moving the file and delete it instead\", \"target_dir\", alertingOrgDir, \"org_id\", orgId, \"error\", err, \"file\", fileName)\n                        deleteFile(fileName)\n                        return\n                }\n                err := os.Rename(filepath.Join(alertingDir, fileName), filepath.Join(alertingOrgDir, fileName))\n                if err != nil {\n                        migrator.Logger.Error(\"Failed to move alertmanager configuration file to organization.\", \"source_dir\", alertingDir, \"target_dir\", alertingOrgDir, \"org_id\", orgId, \"error\", err, \"file\", fileName)\n                        deleteFile(fileName)\n                }\n        }\n\n        entries, err := os.ReadDir(alertingDir)\n        if err != nil {\n                if !os.IsNotExist(err) {\n                        keys := make([]string, 0, len(knownFiles))\n                        for key := range knownFiles {\n                                keys = append(keys, key)\n                        }\n                        migrator.Logger.Warn(\"Failed to clean up alerting directory. There may be files that are not used anymore.\", \"path\", alertingDir, \"files_to_delete\", keys, \"error\", err)\n                }\n        }\n\n        for _, entry := range entries {\n                _, known := knownFiles[entry.Name()]\n                if known {\n                        if orgId == 0 {\n                                deleteFile(entry.Name())\n                        } else {\n                                moveFile(entry.Name())\n                        }\n                }\n        }\n}\n\nfunc (u *upgradeNgAlerting) SQL(migrator.Dialect) string {\n        return codeMigration\n}"

"package ualert\n\nimport (\n        \"fmt\"\n        \"time\"\n\n        \"github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/util/xorm\"\n\n        \"github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator\"\n)\n\n// typeKey is a vendored migration.typeKey.\nvar typeKey = \"currentAlertingType\"\n\n// AlertingType is a vendored migration.store.AlertingType.\ntype alertingType string\n\nconst (\n        Legacy          alertingType = \"Legacy\"\n        UnifiedAlerting alertingType = \"UnifiedAlerting\"\n)\n\n// CreateOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries creates kv store entries for each organization if the migration has been run.\n// This is needed now that we've changed the semantics of data loss when upgrading / rolling back. If a user who previously\n// upgraded were to rollback and upgrade again without clean_upgrade, then since they don't have org-level migrated states\n// it will attempt to upgrade their orgs as if they had never upgraded before. This will almost definitely fail with\n// duplicate key errors.\n//\n// In addition, this changes the entry for orgId=0 to be better named as it no longer tracks whether the\n// migration has been run, but rather the current alerting type of Grafana; Legacy or UnifiedAlerting. This is used to\n// detect transitions between Legacy and UnifiedAlerting by comparing to the desired type in the configuration.\nfunc CreateOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries(mg *migrator.Migrator) {\n        mg.AddMigration(\"copy kvstore migration status to each org\", &createOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries{})\n\n        // Adds back the entry for orgId=0 if it doesn't exist. This is not strictly necessary, but\n        // helps to cover some issues with createOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries if a grafana instance on UA is downgraded to before\n        // the split for org-specific migrated statuses.\n        mg.AddMigration(\"add back entry for orgid=0 migrated status\", &addBackAnyOrgMigratedEntry{})\n}\n\ntype createOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries struct {\n        migrator.MigrationBase\n}\n\nfunc (c createOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries) SQL(migrator.Dialect) string {\n        return codeMigration\n}\n\nfunc (c createOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries) Exec(sess *xorm.Session, mg *migrator.Migrator) error {\n        var anyOrg int64 = 0\n        migrated := kvStoreV1Entry{\n                OrgID:     &anyOrg,\n                Namespace: &KVNamespace,\n                Key:       &migratedKey,\n        }\n        has, err := sess.Table(\"kv_store\").Get(&migrated)\n        if err != nil {\n                return err\n        }\n\n        if !has {\n                mg.Logger.Debug(\"No migrated status in kvstore, nothing to set\")\n                return nil\n        }\n\n        // Rename old entry key and value.\n        val := Legacy\n        if migrated.Value == \"true\" {\n                val = UnifiedAlerting\n        }\n        if _, err := sess.Table(\"kv_store\").Where(\"id = ?\", migrated.ID).Update(&kvStoreV1Entry{\n                Key:   &typeKey,\n                Value: string(val),\n        }); err != nil {\n                mg.Logger.Error(\"failed to rename org migrated status in kvstore\", \"err\", err)\n                return err\n        }\n\n        var orgs []struct {\n                ID int64 `xorm:\"id\"`\n        }\n        if err := sess.SQL(\"select id from org\").Find(&orgs); err != nil {\n                return err\n        }\n\n        if len(orgs) == 0 {\n                mg.Logger.Debug(\"no orgs, nothing to set in kvstore\")\n                return nil\n        }\n\n        for _, org := range orgs {\n                id := org.ID\n                entry := kvStoreV1Entry{\n                        OrgID:     &id,\n                        Namespace: &KVNamespace,\n                        Key:       &migratedKey,\n                        Value:     migrated.Value,\n                        Created:   migrated.Created,\n                        Updated:   migrated.Updated,\n                }\n                if _, errCreate := sess.Table(\"kv_store\").Insert(&entry); errCreate != nil {\n                        mg.Logger.Error(\"failed to insert org migration status to kvstore\", \"err\", errCreate)\n                        return fmt.Errorf(\"failed to insert org migration status to kvstore: %w\", errCreate)\n                }\n        }\n\n        return nil\n}\n\ntype addBackAnyOrgMigratedEntry struct {\n        migrator.MigrationBase\n}\n\nfunc (c addBackAnyOrgMigratedEntry) SQL(migrator.Dialect) string {\n        return codeMigration\n}\n\nfunc (c addBackAnyOrgMigratedEntry) Exec(sess *xorm.Session, mg *migrator.Migrator) error {\n        var anyOrg int64 = 0\n        migratedEntries := make([]kvStoreV1Entry, 0)\n        cond := kvStoreV1Entry{\n                Namespace: &KVNamespace,\n                Key:       &migratedKey,\n        }\n        err := sess.Table(\"kv_store\").Find(&migratedEntries, &cond)\n        if err != nil {\n                return err\n        }\n\n        if len(migratedEntries) == 0 {\n                mg.Logger.Debug(\"No migrated orgs in kvstore, nothing to set\")\n                return nil\n        }\n\n        migratedStatus := \"false\"\n        for _, migrated := range migratedEntries {\n                if migrated.OrgID != nil && *migrated.OrgID == anyOrg {\n                        mg.Logger.Debug(\"Already have migrated status for orgid=0, nothing to set\")\n                        return nil\n                }\n                // All org entries should have the same value. If, somehow, they don't, we set it to true if any orgs are migrated.\n                // This is because assuming an org is migrated when it isn't is less bad as force_migration check exists.\n                if migrated.Value == \"true\" {\n                        migratedStatus = \"true\"\n                }\n        }\n\n        now := time.Now()\n        if _, err := sess.Table(\"kv_store\").Insert(&kvStoreV1Entry{\n                OrgID:     &anyOrg,\n                Namespace: &KVNamespace,\n                Key:       &migratedKey,\n                Value:     migratedStatus,\n                Created:   now,\n                Updated:   now,\n        }); err != nil {\n                mg.Logger.Error(\"failed to insert orgid=0 migrated status in kvstore\", \"err\", err)\n                return err\n        }\n        return nil\n}"
